<script type="text/javascript">


var persistentCookieExpireL = 2592000000;
var wcPersistent = readBrowserCookie('WC_PERSISTENT');
var wcUserActivity = getUserIdFromUserActivityCookie();

var status = "";
var userId = "";
//Authenticated user
if(readCookie("THD_USERSTATUS") == "1"){
	status = "authenticated";
	userId=	wcUserActivity;
}//Guest user
else if(wcPersistent == "" &&  wcUserActivity!= "-1002"){
		status = "guest";
		userId= wcUserActivity;
} //Recognized user
else if (wcPersistent != "" && wcUserActivity!= "-1002" ){
		status = "recognized";
		userId = wcUserActivity;
}
else {
	//Default status is anonymous
	status = "anonymous";
	userId = "-1002";
}

_hddata["custStatus"]= status;
_hddata["customerID"]=userId;
</script>

<script language="javascript">
var url4;
function findCategoryUrl(url1){	
	if(url1.indexOf("/h_d1") > -1){
		url1= url1.substr(0,url1.indexOf("/h_d1"));
		if(url1.length>=url1.lastIndexOf("/")+1)
		{
			url1 = url1.substr(url1.lastIndexOf("/")+1);
		}
	}
	url4 = "Flyout-"+url1;
}
</script>

var fed_confValidate;
fed_confValidate = fed_ciurl.indexOf("OrderOKView");
var fed_scripttag = document.createElement('script');

	fed_scripttag.src=fed_CIcart;
} else if ( fed_confValidate > -1){	
	fed_scripttag.src=fed_CIconfirmation;

	fed_scripttag.src=fed_CIsecure;

<script type="text/javascript">
	function getOverlay()
	{
		var elm = document.getElementsByTagName("body")[0];
		var _width = elm.offsetWidth
		var _height = elm.offsetHeight
		var _top = elm.offsetTop
		var _left = elm.offsetLeft
		var overlay = document.getElementById('overLayDiv');
		overlay.style.width = _width + "px"
		overlay.style.height = _height + "px"
		overlay.style.position = "absolute"
		overlay.style.background = "#666666"
		overlay.style.top = _top + "px"
		overlay.style.left = _left + "px"
		overlay.style.filter = "alpha(opacity=50)"
		overlay.style.opacity = "0.5"
		overlay.style.mozOpacity = "0.5"
		overlay.style.zIndex = "1000"
		return overlay;
	}
	// this method will display the popup
	function openMsgLayer1()
	{
		
		self.scrollTo(0, 0);     		
		var elm = document.getElementsByTagName("body")[0];
		var layer = document.getElementById('cardInfo');
		layer.style.left = (elm.offsetWidth/4) + "px"
		layer.style.top = 100 + "px"
		layer.style.height = 270 + "px"
		layer.style.width = 550 + "px"
		layer.style.zIndex = "1001"
		disableDiv();
		layer.style.display = 'block';
		
	}

	// this method will disable the main div
	function disableDiv()
	{
		document.getElementsByTagName("body")[0].appendChild(getOverlay())
	}	
	
	function closeConfMsgLayer1()
	{
		var layer = document.getElementById('cardInfo');
		layer.style.display = 'none';
		enableDiv();
		
		window.location = ''

	}
	
	function enableDiv()
	{
		var overLay = document.getElementById('overLayDiv');
		document.getElementsByTagName("body")[0].removeChild(overLay)
	}

	if(readCookie("THD_AUTOLOCINTERCEPT") == '1'){
		javaScript:openMsgLayer1();
	}

</script>
